<date>1615570057739<//date><username>Matt Francis< /username><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
I had no teeth on top, and only 8 teeth on the bottom. My lower teeth were completely broken and  Rotted. I am absolutely terrified of the dentist. My experience with clear choice was nothing less amazing!! They really do care about their patients,  and make you feel like family. Dr O and his team are hands down the best there is. My surgery was fantastic and I had very little pain afterwards,  matter of fact I was able to just treat the pain with  Ibuprofen. I just got my final set of teeth yesterday and I was in tears! Dr O gave me my smile back along with opening the door to a whole new world of food. I so recommend them to anyone who is suffering the embarrassing sight of missing teeth or like me having no teeth for almost 18 yrs. For a while I had full dentures, but still found myself unable to eat alot of foods, and often times  Choked while eating, so I just didn't wear them. Not to mention how uncomfortable they really were. My teeth feel like my real teeth. I can now eat whatever I want and have my self confidence and self esteem back! Thank you to the entire staff for helping on this adventure!<//review>

Yesterday I had my All On 4 surgery.  The steps leading up to the procedure and the surgery itself far exceeded my expectations.  My new teeth are beautiful and I wish to thank the excellent doctors and support staff at Clear Choice San Diego for my new smile.

Update -- Received my final set of teeth today.  I'm a retired City of San Diego Equip Tec who specialized in repairing equipment of many different makes and sizes.  I consider my new teeth to be  very precisely made. They remind me of my younger days when I had a full set of teeth. Simply amazing!  Dr. Khatami and his staff were a pleasure to work with.

My mom is 69 and unfortunately has neglected her teeth for most of her life. As a young girl she had a horrible experience at a dentist office and developed a fear of dentists. The combination of this fear and of course putting her children's care over her own lead to the deterioration of her teeth. I knew her teeth were bad but it wasn't until she lost one of her front teeth and we made a trip to the dentist that I really understood the severity of her situation.

We went to a "traditional" dentist and walked away with close to a years worth of appointments. I knew right then that this process would never work. I could possibly get my mom to the first and maybe even the second appointment but after that it would be a struggle.

That is when my family found Clear Choice. My brother and I went to a seminar to learn more about this company, the procedure and if in fact it was true that someone could walk away with a new set of teeth . Well, it was TRUE.

<name>Vinh Huynh< /name>< review>
I have not tried other places to compare, but I chose A-1 because it felt more secure and protected after reading reviews on other places. There is a secure, gated fence, and security alerts (supposedly) if someone access your unit w/o entering the code. It's not a 24 hr watch, but it is better than nothing.

I preferred a drive in unit for ease of moving in and out, but none were available. These are probably hot commodities. My unit was on the 3rd floor. However, they do provide flat-bed carts to help move (and these helped out tremendously. Their elevator is also humongous to fit big items. All in all, it was not as much of a burden as I thought.

Having read previous reviews, I understood when they raise their rent so I was not surprised when it happened. It is something that they do not advertise, but will answer if you inquire about it.

Throughout all my visits, the staff has been courteous whenever I needed to interact with them. I'd recommend this place for anyone considering a storage unit.< /review>

I started my search for storage by using online reviews.  With a little leverage on locations, I soon found my attention drawn to A-1 Storage High Street.  I asked for a space quote online, and found it reasonable. When I came looking for storage , I saw this place close to alameda bridge and I thought this place was very nice and huge. On the tour of the property with one of the friendly associates , I was informed of the security standards they have , accommodating hours (6am - 10pm access hours) , available push carts & a kiosk to make payments anytime ! The service & facility won me over and I came to rent the next week . The process was fast , easy and all rules & regulations were very informative . I plan on staying here a long time ; its a great place to store my personal belongings ! Thumbs up :)< /text>

<response>{'time': 1558634402222, 'text': "Thank you for your recent review of your visit at The Kickin Crab. We hope you enjoy the ambiance and food. We look forward to serving you again soon. BTW we'd be greatly appreciated if you can post on Yelp too. Thanks again Anthony."}<//response><user>107432612639662617077<//user>< review>
The Kickin' Crab is a seafood restaurant with locations scattered around California. This location has a good sized dining area full of bright colors with long tables which makes it ideal for groups. Seafood can be expensive and crab is usually very expensive. Considering that, the prices here are not unreasonable but they are not what I would consider inexpensive. They offer a large variety of crab dishes including large crab buckets that can cost anywhere from $50 to over $70 (depends on market price for crab). Crab isn't all they do though. I have had their seafood fettuccine which comes with shrimp, clams and muscles (still in the shell) with a mildly spiced Cajun cream sauce. It was delicious and I highly recommend it. For a small chain restaurant that happens to be tucked into a corner of a strip mall, this place really impresses. Be prepared to spend more money than you normally would at a restaurant tucked into a strip mall but if you like seafood, it will be worth it.<//review>

<text>Went with family, they got fish tacos and the garlic butter trout dinner, I got fried shrimp and fries. The trout was pretty good and my grandpa enjoyed the rice pilaf although I didn't try it. The biggest flaw was the fish tacos, they were pretty meager with pieces of fish no bigger than your thumb, and more salsa than fish. For the price and considering it was probably more if an appetizer the shrimp wasn't too offensive but a bit disappointing. Tasted ok just a bit overcooked but they have good shoestring fries and free sauces to go along with it.

Normally at a place like this we'd get the seafood boil and it looked quite good, but didn't have time to go for the full mess. The place was clean and the service was friendly but you can tell they are still in the growing pains of opening. Giving it a 3 star now but I fully expect it to get better over time.< /text>< pictures>

<Review>When we made to decision to start looking for a new apartment we started by making a list of important amenities and features that were necessary for our family. At the top of the list was dog friendly, location, spacious rooms, washer and washer, dishwasher, and pool.

After driving around the neighborhoods we wanted to stay in and hours of research online, we decided to take a couple of tours. Avana Almaden was at the top of our list for many reasons. After physically touring the community and meeting with Nathaniel several times (he answered all of our questions and was so friendly) we decided it was the right place for us.

We had some reservations. The community is quite large and we wondered about the noise level. We had some concerns about parking availability (the street parking always looked so full). And we noticed that there are more than a couple homeless camps nearby and we were a little hesitant to move our family so close to them (for many reasons- including that we have kids that walk to and from school, normally).

To our surprise, the community is very quiet and peaceful and thus far we have not had a single issue with finding parking- even when we have late evening commitments. As far as the homeless community, we have yet to even see them around the complex. Our sons have ventured out to walk and bike ride with no problems (they are 13 and 15 years old).

Overall, we could not be happier with our choice the make Avana Almaden our home. We would highly recommend this community and are so grateful to Nathaniel and the leasing team! Through all of this the office manager was unfriendly and unhelpful, she went as far as to blame us. We had to ask for an extension on our lease, due to having a hard time finding a new place to live (you know what I mean if you are a SJ native). As we were moving out, I realized how bad the mice infestation had been. Along the walls behind the furniture we don't move, was mouse droppings and pee. I was mortified...so much that I left all my food in the fridge! After filing a complaint and having our lawyers send out a letter, they blamed us and painted us as bad tenants.

Go ahead and move here, I'm sure it's not common practice, because the folks that work in the office are very friendly and personable.
